et le met on aucune fois au leu qui saine a copement des voines, et as arteres, et aucune fois reont selonc ceste grant forme:	And let it remain one time in its healthy position where all veins are properly connected and the arteries too, never once conforming to this grand form:
Aucune fois enflent les mameles d’aucuns homes quant cil encomencent estre corrumput, tant qu’eles semblent mameles de feme;	Never do the breasts of some men swell when they begin to rot, until they seem like breasts of women;

puis escorche la graisse, et emple la plaie de medicine enjanrant char, puis assemble les .ij. levres de la plaie a costure, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee;	Then strip off the fat, and apply medicine to the wound that stimulates healing tissue, then join together the two sides of the wound for stitching, and continue with the treatment until it is healed.
et se li mamele cline aval, et est amolie por sa grandor si com il avient as femmes, si la fent en .ij. costelz desus, par .ij. semblans fendures;	And if the mammary gland sags down, and is flattened by its size especially like in women, so that she divides them into two lobes, by two similar fissures;

dou chancre	and the sore
Nos avons dit en la division les semblances de chancre, et coment on i doit ovrer par medicines, et coment on doit eschuer la cure de fer; et disons le chancre enjanreit en la marris, et grant cautele a en la cure, et dirent li ancien que quant chancres est en leu ou on le puet raier si com chancre qui est em mameles, et en la cuixe, et en semblans leus, et le doit tout oster quant il est en l’encomencement; et quant il est grans et anciens, si ne covient mie que tu l’aproches, car je n’en poi onques nul saner; ne nulz n’en sana onques devant moi.	We have discussed the appearances of a sore in division and how to address it with medicine and how to avoid iron treatment. Let us discuss an ingrowing sore, and there is great caution needed in its treatment; the old say that when sores are found on skin or can be scraped off such as under breasts and in cooking areas, and those common places, they should all be removed at their beginning; but for large and old ones, it's not suitable to approach them, because I have never known anyone to recover from such cases; no one has ever recovered from these types of sores before me.
Et li ovraiges, quant il est en leu ou on le puet oster, si com nos avons dit, est que tu purge aucune fois le malaide de cole noire; puis le fai sainier s’il ait manifeste repletion, puis afaite le malaide .i. boin leu por faire l’ovraige; puis giete tes oncines ou chancre, et le cheve de toutes pars, et l’oste de toutes pars sens rien laissier; et laisse corre le sanc tout fuer, et espreint bien le leu a ta main ou a aucune chose, et se li decorremens de sanc te fait contraire de l’incision de l’artere ou de la voine, si le cauterize tant que li sans soit estainchiez; puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And in the case of ingrowing sores, when they can be scraped off as we have said, it is that you cleanse the diseased area of black scabs once. Then let the surgeon know if there's visible swelling, then prepare the diseased area to be open - that means making sure it's clean and clear skin ready for opening; then remove your warts or sores from all around, and scrape everything off without leaving anything behind; and leave no wound open, press well on the wound with your hand or any object, and if the bleeding stops opposite the cut of the artery or vein, cauterize until there's no more bleeding; then treat it further until it heals.
de ydropisie	Of cautery from fire command the sick person to let the hairs grow long and even; and if they prick at their base, hold the eyes steady so they do not move until they grow.
Nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’idropisie, et en queil maniere li assemblee de l’aigue est faite, et les signes de chescune semblance, et la cure qui est faite par medicines, et cele qui est curee par fer: si est eclites soulement; et ne doit on touchier de fer en ces .ij. semblances: c’est a savoir, tympanites et yposarche, car c’est mortelz chose; donques quant tu medicines ceste semblance de ydropisie qui est apelee «eclites» de medicines, et li cure ne profite, si regarde se li malaides est foibles, ou s’il ait autre maladie que ydropisie, si com toust et solution de ventre et semblans choses; si n’i touchier de fer, car il i a doutance; et se tu vois le malaide de fort vertut, et il n’a autre maladie que ydropisie soulement, et il n’est mie trop jones ne trop vielz, si dois ensi ovrer:	We have discussed the appearances of dropsy in division, and how the assembly of water is made, and the signs for each appearance, and the treatment that is done with medicines, and that which is treated with iron: these are all clearly detailed; and should we not use iron in these two appearances: one is known as tympanites and the other is dropsy, since it is a deadly matter; therefore when you medicate this appearance of dropsy called "dropsy" from medicines, and the treatment doesn't help, if you notice that the patient's condition is weak, or they have another disease besides dropsy, such as stomach solution and similar conditions; then do not use iron, because there is doubt in this case; and when you see a very green color on the patient, and they only have dropsy without any other disease, and if they are neither too young nor too old, then proceed like this to operate:
lieve le malaide droit sus tes mains, et li ministres presse le ventre em boutant l’aigue a la plus basse partie dou pis, puis pren le spatumile espinous selonc ceste forme: Et soit trenchans de .ij. pars. a pointe, et toutevoie ne soit mie si entrans qu’il puist venir jusc’a l’intestine quant on le fiche ens, et ne le puist blecier;	Lift the patient's side with your hands, and have the assistant press the stomach in the lower part near the ankle while pouring water downwards. fai ce aucun jor, et te garde de foloier tant qu’il ni demore mais c’un poc d’aigue. de l’estopement de la verge	On circumcision
Aucune fois naissent enfant qui n’ont point de pertus en la verge, ou li pertus est petis, ou il n’est mie en son leu. puis leve la plaie d’aigue et d’aisil et de seil, et li aide en toutes les manieres que tu seis, tant qu’il soit sanez; et covient que toutes les oures que tu le cures, que tu li lie les .ij. cuisses, et assemble les medicines sus le leu.	Then cleanse the wound with water and salt and soap, and assist in all ways that you can see fit, until it heals; and when treating every injury, tie the legs together and place the medicines on top of it.
Et se li piere est petite, et ele est ou conduit de la verge, et fichie ens, et li urine ne puet issir; si le cure de ceu que je dis ainsois, que tu lou tailles maintes fois, est on escusez de la taille per ceste cure. Je ai ja ce proveit ensi.	And if the stone is small and it's inside the urethra, causing urine to not be able to come out; when treating as I have described, cut many times and excuse the cuts due to this treatment. I have already found this effective.
Pren .i. foret de fer selonc ceste forme et soit a .iij. angles fichiees en .i. tison:	Take one piece of iron according to this form, and have it pierced at three points on one point.
puis pren .i. fil et lou lie entor la verge desoz la piere, si qu’ele ne puist venir arrier en la vessie; puis boute le foret en la verge legierement, tant qu’il viegne a la piere; et torne le foret a ta main en la piere poc et poc, tant que tu puisses percier la piere d’autre part; si venra tantost li urine, puis presse ta main sus ceu qui est demorez de la piere qui est dedens la verge. Si est tantost brisie, et saut fuer avec l’urine, et est garis li malaides;	Then take one thread and tie it around the shaft of the penis so that it does not come back into the bladder; then insert the iron rod in the penis gently until it reaches the stone; and twist the iron rod in your hand on the stone little by little, until you can pierce the stone from another side; if urine starts coming out quickly, then press your hand on what is left of the stone inside the penis. If it breaks quickly, and there is urine with the action, and heals the patient;
et se tu ne pues ce faire por aucune chose qui le deffent, si lie .i. fil desoz la piere et .i. autre desus, puis fent la verge endroit la piere entre les .ij. liiens, puis l’estrai fuer, et deslie lou liien, et mundifie lou sanc congeleit qui est en la plaie; et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you cannot do this for any reason that prevents it, tie one thread around the stone and another above it, then place the penis between the two threads over the stone, then forcefully pull on the penis, untie the thread, and cleanse the congealed blood in the wound; and treat until it is healed.
de la piere des femmes	of the stone in women
Poc avient que piere soit enjanree en femmes, et s’il avient aucune fois, si est li cure grief, et est deffendut por .iij. choses: l’une est que per aventure li femme est vierge; et li seconde est c’on ne puet trover femme bien saichant qui se descuevre as mires, meismement quant elle est caste.	Sometimes a stone occurs in women, and if it happens even once, this is treated with the utmost care, and precautions are taken against three things: one is that perhaps the woman is a virgin; and the second is that one cannot find a woman who knows how to conduct herself properly when looking into mirrors, even if she is chaste.
Et li tierce maniere si est que par aventure on ne puet trover femme bien saichant en cest art de mains; et li quarte maniere si est que li piere de la femme si est plus em parfont que li piere de l’ome, por coi il i couvient faire plus parfonde taille, et grant paour i a.	And the third way could be that by chance one cannot find a woman who is well skilled in this art of hands; and the fourth way is that the stone in a woman is closer to the surface than a man's stone, for which reason it requires a deeper cut and considerable fear arises.
Et se necessitez semont a ceu, si covient que tu preignes une mieresse bien sachant, et a poines la trueve on, et se tu n’en trueves, point si quier .i. caste mire subtil; et li presente une baile bien saige en la vie des femmes, ou une femme qui saiche une partie de l’art, et li comande qu’ele faice ceu que tu li comandes de l’inquisicion de la piere;	And if necessity pushes you to this, then it is necessary that you seek out someone well skilled, and touch their knowledge with truthfulness, or if you do not find even one chaste person who tells the truth, choose instead a cunning old woman in women's affairs, or a woman who knows part of the art, and command her to perform as you instruct on the examination of the stone;
et regarde mout bien se li femme est vierge: adonques li covient bouter son doit ou fondement et querir la piere; et s’ele la trueve, si la constraigne desoz son doit, et li recomande qu’elle boute son doit ou con la malaide, et quiere et presse sa main senestre sus la vessie forment.	And very carefully observe if the woman is a virgin: then it's necessary to press her womb or foundation and look for the stone; and if she finds it, make her place herself on her back over her womb and take it; and when she has found it, keep her to press it down with her hand as closely onto her abdomen.
S’elle la trueve, si covient qu’elle la mueve de greit en greit des l’entree de la vessie jusque desoz, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la cuisse; puis cope sus la piere en la racine de la cuisse encontre le mileu dou con, lai ou il est mues apparilliet, et sent la piere en celle partie; et ne mueve son doi desus la piere ou desoz, et soit li taille au premier petite;	If she finds it, then it's proper for her to move the stone from side to side while entering the bladder up until under it, as long as she reaches the root of the thigh; then press against the stone at the root of the thigh opposite the inside of the hip, where it's slightly larger and feels the stone in that area; and do not move her hand above or underneath the stone, but make sure to stop after a small movement.
puis boute lou rait en la taille, se tu sens la piere si acroi la plaie tant que li piere puisse issir fuer, et saiches que maintes manieres de pieres sont: c’est a savoir, petites et grans et aspres et souez, longes et reondes, et qui ont rains. si saiches les semblances por savoir l’issue.	Then press on the stomach, if you feel the stone increase the wound until the stone can come out forcefully, and know that there are many types of stones: this means small and large, hard and smooth, long and round, and some have bumps. If you understand these characteristics to know the exit point.
Et se li sans te vaint, si met au leu vitriole broiet, et li tien une houre tant que li sans soit estainchiez; puis revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer, et aies des estrumens que je t’ai dit en l’estraction de la piere as homes por toi aidier en ton oevre;	And if it doesn't heal with you, apply vitriol and keep it there for an hour until the wound is healed; then return to your work until the stone is removed, and use instruments that I have told you about in removing stones for helping you in your task.
et se li sans te vaint, et c’est de l’artere qui est copee, si met la poudre sus le leu et l’estrain de tentes et de bendelz, et ne rencomencier plus ceu, et laisse la piere et ne la traire mie, que par aventure morroit li malaide; puis cure la plaie.	And if the wound doesn't heal and it's an artery that's been cut, apply powder on the wound and bind with cloths and hemp, and do not repeat this step again, leave the stone and don't try to remove it, in case accidentally it kills the patient; then treat the wound.
Et quant li chalor dou sanc est apaisie, et li leus porrist, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer.	And when the heat of blood has been calmed and the wounds have healed, then return to your work until the stone is removed.
de hernie carnouse	Of fatty hernia
Ramice aquouse n’est autre chose que assemblee de moistor ou blanc syfac, qui est desoz lou keur des coions, que contient l’uef; et est apelez «syfac», et aucune fois est proprement en la toile de l’uef, si c’on cuide que ce soit .i. autre oef; et c’est li cuir dou coion entre lou blanc syfac que nos avons dit; et ceu n’avient se poc non.	Of watery phlegm is nothing other than a gathering of moisture or white sputum, which resides within the folds of the testicles, contained in the egg; and it is called 'sputum', and has no proper place within the fabric of the egg, should one think it's another kind; and this is the skin under the testicle where we have spoken; and this does not have a pore.
Et li generation de cest ramice si est de foibleteit que vient as coions, et est espandue celle matiere.	And the production of such phlegm is so weak that it comes to the testicles, and spreads this material.
Et aucune fois si vient de percussion sus les coions, et ceste moistor si a maintes colors: ou c’est color declinans a jaunice, ou c’est sans rouge, ou noir, ou aquous blans, et ce avient plus;	And it never comes from striking the testicles, and this moisture can have many colors: or it becomes declining to jaundice, or it is without redness, or black, or aqueous white, and this happens more often.
et ce sont li signe de conoistre ceste assemblee, car s’elle est ou blanc syfac que nos avons dit, si est li apostemes reons, .i. poc lonc si com li figure d’un oef, et n’apert mie li coions, car il a moistor tout entor.	And these are the signs to recognize this assembly, for if it is or white like we have said, then the abscesses are present, that is, one as long as an egg figure, and does not open within the skin, because there is moisture throughout.
Et s’il a moistor en la propre toile, si est li apostemes reons avec une partie de l’uef, et por ceu pense on que c’est uns autres oef;	And if there is moisture in the inner lining, then the abscesses are present with part of an egg, and because of this, one might think it's another egg;
et se li moistor est entre le cuir des coions et le blanc syfac, si le sent om bien; donques quant tu vues savoir la color de la moistor, si esprueve a tout l’intromissoire quarreit, de coi li forme est ci devant.	And if the moisture is between the skin of the testicle and the white part, you can feel it well; therefore, when you see to know the color of the moisture, you test everything in the incision area, from which the shape is as described before.
Selonc ceu donques qui vient aprés l’intromissoire, juge de ceu qui est dedens.	Following this, as those who come after the initial introduction, judge according to what is inside.
Et quant nos la curons par fer, si covient que li malaides soit sainiez selonc som pooir et la repletion de son cors; puis le sovine sus son dos, sus une chose un poc haute, et met desoz lui mout de drapelz;	And when we cure it with a iron, the patient should be treated according to our skill and their body's capacity; then they should be laid upon their back, slightly elevated, and blankets should be placed under them.
puis sié sus sa senestre, et comande au ministre qu’il sié a destre, et estende la verge a l’un des .ij. costelz dou keur des coions;	Then sit on their left side, and command the minister to sit on the right, stretching out one arm under one of the patient's ribs towards the heart area.
puis pren le spatumile leit, et cope le cuir des coions parmi leu dou lonc jusque delez lou poignil, et soit ta fendure toute droite en devisant le cuir des coions jusc’a syfac blanc, et l’escorche subtilment selonc tom pooir;	Then take the spit and coat the skin around the ribs with it along its length until below the elbow, and make sure to cut the incision straight across through the skin until you reach the white fat, and gently remove the overlying layer of skin according to your ability.
puis perce lou syfac plain d’aigue a .i. large pertus, et estrai toute l’aigue, et puis met tes oncines, et estent lou syfac amont; et ne touchier le keur des coions, mais que le syfac soulement; cope tout ou par pieces meismement le costeit de lui subtil, que se tu ne le copes bien saigement, si revenra li aigue;	Then pierce the wet spot fully with an awl of size one and a half inches across, remove all water, then insert your forceps, have the wetness up front; and do not touch the center of the kidneys, but only the wet area; take out the entire rib or piece by piece from his backside, since if you don't extract it carefully enough, water will return.
et se l’uef saut fuer a ton oevre, si le ramoinne en son leu quant tu avras acomplit l’uevre dou syfac; puis assemble les .ij. leivres dou keur des coions a une costure, puis le cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the egg jumps to your work, then reset it in its place once you have completed the work on the wet spot; then join the two halves of the kidney's center with a stitch, and then treat it like other wounds until it heals completely.
Et se tu trueves l’uef corromput d’autre maladie, si covient que tu lies les vasselz que sont suspensoire, en doutant le decorrement de sanc; puis cope le coion a tout le suspensoire, et estrai l’uef, et le cure si com nos avons dit.	And if you find the egg corrupted by another disease, it is necessary that you tie the ligaments that are suspended, fearing the bleeding; then cut through the scrotum up to the suspension point, remove the egg, and treat it as we have said before.
Et se aigue est assemblee en .ij. parties ensamble, saiches que ce sont .ij. ramices; si cope l’autre partie si com tu as fait la premiere igalment, puis essue lou sanc, et met en la plaie lainne moillie en oile roset;	And if the wound is formed into two joined parts, know that these are two branches; so handle the other part in the same way as you did the first equally, then bleed it out and apply wet wool soaked in rose oil to the wound.
et met defuer autre laine moillie en vin et en oile, et met sus les .ij. coions, et met desus drapelz doublés, et le lie sus a tout le liien qui est selonc ceste forme:	and apply another layer of wet wool in wine and oil, and place it over the two stumps, then cover with folded cloths, and secure them above following this form.
Puis pren .ij. drapelz, et les emple de laine charpie selonc ceste semblance et soient assemblez par cousture en la gorle des braies, et li uns des chiés preigne sus le fondement jusc’au dos, et li autres a la partie dou poignil; et li autre dui chief sus les .ij. angres, et soit toute assemblee li restreinture en la boucle dou braier;	Then take two cloths and fold them with striped wool according to this pattern and have them joined by sewing in the waistband of the trousers, and one end of the shoulder goes down to the foundation up to the back, and the other at the part near the wrist; and the second neck above the two corners, and make sure the tightening is inside the loop of the garter.
et aucune fois est medicinee ceste ramice de cautere en leu de taille de fer, et est que tu preignes .i. cautere cultellaire subtil, et cope le cuir des coions, et soit eschaufez si com nos avons dit, si que li syfac blanc que contient l’aigue est descovers;	And never is this cure of the fire cautery in the size of iron, and you take one small surgical instrument cautery, and cut the skin of the legions, and heat it up as we have said, so that the white fluid contained in the water becomes revealed;
si pren lou cautere selonc ceste forme, et perce celui syfac as oncines, et l’escorche a cest subtil cautere chaut:	Take the cautery according to this form, and pierce that white spot like oncinia (a unit of measurement), and scorch with that subtle fire tool:
Et lou cope en toutes les manieres que tu pues, tant que tu esraiches tout; et garde que li feus ne touche l’uef; et saiches que ceste oevre est plus salve; et mues gardans de decorrement de sanc, et muedres que li ovraiges de taille;	And cut in all the ways you can until you exhaust everything; and make sure that the fire does not touch the egg; and know that this operation is more safe; and watch out for bleeding, and be aware of the size of cuts.
et se nulle chose te fait contraire, ou aposteme chaus ou decorremens de sanc ou autre chose, si cure ce qui te fait contraire, selonc ceu qui est devant dit.	And if nothing opposes you, or if pus comes out or bleeding starts, or any other thing happens, then treat what is opposing you according to the one who spoke before.
Et se li malaides est paourous, et ne vuet atendre cest ovraige por son horribleteit, si amenistre perforation, si com je te di, et est que quant tu es bien certains par les significations que nos avons dit que ramice aquouse est lai,	And if the patient is fearful and cannot bear to undergo this work due to its horribleness, then perform a puncture, as I have told you, and know that when you are well convinced by the meanings we have explained that watery matter is there,
si fai seoir le malaide sus .i. siege leveit; puis perce l’aposteme an la partie desoz a tout le spatumile large, et met la perforation dou lonc dou cors; et soit larges li pertus, si que toute li aigue corre fuer;	And make the patient sit on a raised seat; then puncture the abscess in the part below at all the broad pus-filled area, and make the incision long along the body; and make the holes wide so that all the liquid flows out.
puis met coton sus le leu, et le lie, et laisse por corre le remenant de l’aigue, puis le cure tant que li plaie soit sanee;	Then place cotton on the wound, and bind it, and let the liquid flow away through it, then treat until the wound is healed.
et se li blainche toile ne laisse issir l’aigue en la bouche de la plaie, si covient que tu i boutes une penne ou l’estrument dont on trait l’aigue des ydropiques, de coi li forme est ci devant; et eslarge .i. poc la plaie, et saiches que li aigue revient, et est assemblee aprés .vj. mois ou enqui entor, et quant elle est assemblee si com devant, et ensi passera li malaides ses jors.	And if the whitened cloth does not allow water to escape from the wound's mouth, then it is necessary for you to stuff in a feather or an instrument used to treat the water drops from those with dropsy, which has been described previously; and make the opening one inch wide of the wound, and know that the water returns, and assembles after about seven months or more, and when she returns like before, then this will pass through the disease's days.
de l’aposteme des coions	Regarding the extraction of pus from the testicles
Saiches que en la section de ceste ramice a paor em plusors dispositions, por coi il me semble que mues vaut c’on la laisse;	Know that in this part of the branch there are various ways to cause fear, which is why I think it's better if you let it be.
et je vos dirai l’ovraige et les semblances de l’aposteme.	And I will tell you about how to do it, and what an abscess looks like when cut open.
Je dis donques que maint aposteme vienent ou cors, et meismement as coions; et c’est par mout de cas.	So I say that many abscesses come from thorns or even within the body; and it happens by chance.
C’est a savoir par superfluiteit aigre et ague, qui est espandue as coions, ou de percussion;	This is to know that through excess of sharpness and fever, which spreads in thorns or due to impact;
et est li color de l’aposteme selonc la color dou cors; et ne trueve point de dolor, et est aposteme grief;	And the color of the abscess corresponds to the color of the thorn; and you don't find any pain, it's a thorny abscess;
et par aventure est uns apostemes griés paourous et pierous, et de fuxe color, et aucune fois vient de nout d’artere, ou d’enfleure de voine.	And by chance there may be an abscess filled with pus and stones, of a red color, and it never comes from the heart or inflamed vein.
Quant c’est par nout d’artere, si est conus par la disposition d’aposteme chaut, quant tu la presses a tes dois;	When it's due to an artery, if you recognize it by the location of the pulsating abscess, when you press on it with your fingers;
et ne covient mie que tu i touches.	And it is not right for you to touch it.
Cil qui est fais d’enfleure de voine est conus par sa disposition a l’expression dou touchement des dois,	That which is made of inflamed vein can be identified by its location and the feeling when pressing with your fingers on it,
et puet om bien faire la taille sus ceste semblance, et sus les autres chars;	And can certainly do the measurement on this kind of thing, and on other parts;
et est que tu cope lou keur des coions, puis estent l’uef en haut, et le trai fuer dou blanc syfac, et delivre lou suspensoire de toutes pars de l’uef.	And you must cut the womb of the calf, then it is in the middle part, and the main tendon should be under white skin, and release all suspensory structures from the egg.
Se li uef est ja sodez avec ces chars nees, si covient donques que tu traies l’uef, et lou cope;	If the calf has already been born with these parts attached, then you must remove the calf and its copula.
et s’il est aers au syfac, ou en ceu qui est dedens les vasselz, si covient que tu delivre toute celle tenve, et la cope reondement.	And if it is under the skin or within the vessels, you must release all that tissue and then remove its copula in a circular motion.
Et se li naissance de la char est ou leu derrier, si covient que tu la copes toute, et estrai l’uef, si com nous avons dit.	And if the place of birth of the child is at his rear, it must be that you take all of it, and remove the egg, as we have said.

de l’aposteme des coions	from the abscess of the glands
Cis est uns apostemes envoloupez d’un envoloupement semblant a .i. borjon, avec le mollifiement des coions,	This is an abscess surrounded by a wrapping that resembles half a ring, with the gland swelling.

car par ceu n’i vient point de mal, et se a toz les vasselz vient vis, si covient traire les coions a tout les vasselz;	because this causes no harm, and if all the vessels come into view, then it is necessary to apply the coagulants to all the vessels;
si que li oes ne perde son norrissement por l’incision des vasselz, et sechent et ne se puient aidier.	so that the body does not lose its healing through the incisions of the vessels, and they dry out and cannot be helped.
de la routure dou syfac	Of the rupture of the scrotum
Li avenemens de ceste ramice si est par la section que vient ou syfac, ou l’estension sus le ventre en la partie des angres, por coi li intestine dessendent de celle routure a l’un des coions;	The occurrences of this branch happen through the section that leads to the scrotum or the abdominal expansion in the part of the groin, because the intestines descend from that rupture into one of the testicles.
et ceste routure est ou dou syfac, ou de l’estension de li, et vienent ces .ij. manieres de mout de causes: ou de percussion, ou de saut, ou de braire, ou de levement de grief faix, et par semblans choses;	And this rupture is either at the scrotum or due to the expansion of the belly in the part of the groin. These two ways of happening originate from these four causes: impact, jumping, crying out, lifting of a heavy object, and similar actions.
et li signes quant c’est de l’estension dou syfac, si est qu’il avient poc et poc, en lonc tens, et ne vient mie soudainnement;	And when it's due to the expansion at the scrotum, symptoms occur gradually and over a long period of time, not suddenly.
et est li apostemes igalz jusque vers le parfont, por ceu que li syfac apresse l’intestine.	And the abscesses are even up to around the front side, because pus rushes towards the intestine.
Et li signes est quant c’est de la section dou syfac, qu’elle fait venir a l’encomencement dolor soudaine, et est li apostemes divers apparans, desoz le cuir pres, et c’est por l’issue de l’intestine et le cors au defuer dou syfac.	And the signs are when it comes to cutting across the gland, causing a sudden onset of pain at the beginning, and abscesses appear in various forms, near the skin area, because of the exit route from the intestine and the body beyond the gland.
Et aucune fois dessent li cirbes avec l’intestine, et est retenus enqui, et fait grant dolor soffrir au malaide, meismement quant il est pressez.	And it happens that the lymph nodes descend with the intestine, and are retained therein, causing great suffering to the patient, especially when pressed.
Et en ces cures de fer a paor, por coi il s’en covient eschuir.	And in these times of fear and anxiety, it's advisable to avoid them.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que tu comande ou malaide qu’il ramoine l’intestine a sa main au dedens en la plaie, s’il i puet rentreir;	And the way of performing it is that you instruct the patient to have the diseased part remove the intestines from within through the wound with their hand if they can fit inside.
puis soit sovinez sus son col. entre tes mains, et lieve les cuixes;	then sew up his neck. hold him between your hands and lift his legs;
puis estent le keur au desus, et cope tout le cuir des coions dou lonc;	next stretch the stomach upwards, and peel off all the skin from the belly as long as possible;

Et s’il n’ist fuer si com nos avons dit, si le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit selonc la figure natureil.	And if it doesn't move as we have said, if he twists a little bit by a little bit, until it follows the natural figure.
Car adonques ist il legierement.	Therefore, he should be gently handled.
Et s’il ne vient fuer si com nos avons dit, si pren muscillaige de altee, et oile de sisament, et gomme fondue, et broie tout en .i. mortier;	And if it doesn't act as we have said, take a masticatory stick, and oil of saffron, and gum resin, and melted down gum; grind all of this together in a one-liter mortar;
et met sus la nature de la femme dedens et defuer cest oignement,	and place the body of the woman inside and outside of this ointment,
puis la fai seoir en aigue tede jusque desoz les costelz;	Then make them sit in cold water up to their ribs;
et quant elle est moillifie desoz, se li fai .i. coliere de mirre, et li met desoz, et li laisse une houre;	And when they are thoroughly moistened below, give them one spoonful of turpentine and place it there, leaving it for an hour;
puis la fai seoir sus .i. siege, puis la fai esternuer et estraint sa bouche et son neis, et li preint le ventre legierement, car li enfes saut maintenant.	Then make them sit on a stool, after which have them sneeze and restrain their mouth and nose, and gently massage their abdomen, because the child jumps now.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses genous	From the issue of the child on its knees
Quant li enfes vient en ceste forme, si i mette li baile ses mains poc et poc;	When the child comes in this form, if he places his hands slowly and slowly.

de l’issue de l’enfant qui vient dou large une main pendant	From the birth of the child that emerges with one hand during

de ceste meisme maniere a tout la secondine	In this same manner for all the rest

de l’issue des gemelz	about the birth of twins
Saiches que gemeil naissent maintes fois, et aucune fois en naissent .iij. ou .iiij.; et ceu n’est mie estrainge chose, et poc avient.	Know that twins are born many times, and sometimes three or four at a time; and this is not an uncommon thing, it simply happens.

je sai ceu, qu’il soient multipliiet, et sont desevrez par lou syfac qui les devise, qui est liiez a la boude;	I know this, when they are multiplied, and they are removed by the syphilitic disease which creates them, which is linked to the body;

de plusors enfans	Of several children
Aucune fois sont formez en la marris .i. ou .ij. ou .iij. ou .iiij. ou .v. ou .vj. ou .vij., ou plusors jusc’a .xv., et sont tout formeit en forme d’enfant par le mesurement dou saige glorious,	They are formed in marriage once or twice or three times or four times or five times, and sometimes up to fifteen times, and they are all shaped like a child by the measure of their glory,

de l’enfant mort	From the dead child
Quant tu cures la femme de l’enfant mort ou ventre, si com j’ai dit en la division, et il ne vient fuers, et tu es constrains d’ovraige de mains;	When you treat a woman who has lost her child or is miscarried, as I have explained in the division section, if it does not come out and you are forced to intervene manually;

Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut .i. autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	And I saw a woman who had lost an unborn child in her belly, and later recovered for another one, and the other gave birth to it again.

et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	And let the woman wait long until thus, and it will become somewhat more to her liking.
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	And I remember this chapter only so that if the masters find a strange thing, they know how to give help.
dou ramener la marris a son leu	to bring back the married one to their place
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres; et a .ij. tornans as .ij. chiés des .ij. liiens.	After this comes the form of the presser, to which books are attributed; and for two forms each of four limbs.

Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	The shape of the instrument used to fumigate the woman during the retention of flowers and the second stage is this:

de percier lou fondement	To pierce the base
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	Many infants are born who have not had their base pierced, but instead something subtle and difficult has occurred:

de la fistule dou fondement	from the sinus with its foundation
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des .ij. parties,	Fistulas that come from the base are nodule-like, and grow larger than those that come from under the base or within the space of two parts,

et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans; et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	and these fistulas are perennial; and they are recognized by the fact that there is discharge or windiness when the patient expels, and sometimes one towards another.
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge; et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	And if there are fistulas that reach up to the bladder, and halfway down the penis; and they can reach up to the joint of the leg, and even to the root of the testicles.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	And thus one knows whether a fistula is perennial at its base, and not so.
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	And you bend your index finger or its base, and insert a delicate needle or a spider pin in the puncture where there is no winding.
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou .i. poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	And if it has winding or twist, if you insert a subtle plug, or even a horsehair, as long as you feel the plug or hair on your index finger;
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	And if you do not feel it, and there is no discharge of pus nor wind nor infection, as we have said:
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie; si te haste dou curer.	You will know that she does not pierce at all; if you hasten to cure.
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	And when the fistula is situated right up to the bladder or all the way along where urine leads, if the urine jumps there, and cannot be joined by medicine.
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	If it's punctured up to the knee joint, then the flow comes up to the thigh;
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	If there is no twist and the source of pain lies internally, then it's as if it were within, and it doesn't respond to medicine or by means of application;
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	And for these fistulas that are down to the end, there is no remedy except work and the folly of those who interfere with them.
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit,	In neither the Persian nor the ancient medical practice, there was hope for healing through iron, as I have proven.
et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos; et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	And it is that the patient lies on their back with their hands in your grasp; and you raise their legs up to their hips, and have their thighs leaned towards their belly;
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	Then place an araigne web, or if there's twisting, as long as you know where the web comes from.
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice,	If the patient senses something under the foundation, then it is necessary for you to press your index finger onto that place.
se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet; et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	You can feel then that something has pierced you; and if discovered, or when feeling between your finger and thumb, it indicates she is within you.
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	If there's no bleeding when trying to cut it out, then one cannot heal it.
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	Yet even so, one can certainly heal some of them, but this happens very rarely.
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	and with the help that one provides, if one heats the fine cautery according to the width of the fistula, as was explained before;
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement; et faice ceu .ij. fois ou .iij., tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	And he holds the heated implement in the wound until it reaches beyond the base; and perform this action twice or three times, until you know that these burned things resemble a feather of a bird.
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	And then the salve for moist burns should be applied until that burned thing emerges, then apply the ointment to seal and fuse it.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien. Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	If it is in this manner healthy, it's good. If not, nothing else can be made well;
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	And if it is tested inside and does not pierce up to the root which is or foundation, and in between your thumb and the tent you have a thick covering of flesh or fat, and you see the wound beneath that skin where the covering touches properly.
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	If you intervene at the start of the abscess, hold it steady before the tentacle, and then apply the cautery afterwards, until it reaches the tip of the tentacle;
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra; puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	Then release the tentacle, and it will fall off; then cleanse those hardened spots that resemble a bird's feather, and do not leave any remnants.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	And if the wound does not heal, cut between you and the tissue, then apply fire or medicinal alcohol to it.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble .ij. bones choses: c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	For the fire cauterizations gather two things: these are to know, the scorching of these joined parts, and the suction of blood and the drying out of moisture;
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	Then the treatment of wet bandages or in ground ashes, until his limbs sweat out, and the heat goes into the sweat.
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	Then treat the wound with the application of hard charcoal poultices, and let the dry medicines work.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	For when it is healed, if it heals completely and does not recur.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	And if a sinus comes up just to the full depth of the foundation, and is distant from the body, you should plug its root or foundation, and inquire about it.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre .ij. est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des .iii. manieres:	If you feel the tent, and there are two in the mesh or the liver or heart, or it is almost ready to pierce, but only has a way of fear and hope, by administering one of three methods:
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	or you cauterize it as we have said, or you remove up to the root, or if you can reach with a probe and a cure like at first;
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	and don't go too deep into it, so you don't remove the holding piece which supports the base, and let the evacuations come out willingly through there;
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	then treat it as we have said;
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	By chance if it is healed, or you remove that covering and clean it since it has been cut from the base, either by trial or with another instrument pointed towards it;
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	Then cleanse the flesh in the wound as much as you can;
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement: si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	Then try to heal the wound, and to keep the pus in the lower part of the base: if it's easier for the patient.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere: et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus,	And always perform pus discharges in this manner: and when you puncture the pus pocket, and it's located under the skin above the base.
si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	if you take a tent piercing through the head according to this form:
Et i boute .i. fil tort en .ij., et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	And tie two twisted threads together, and place the tent at both ends of the thread within the tube until it reaches the head.
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	If it is foreign matter at the edge of the base inside, then extract the thread from this twisted one, in such a way that you are holding your tool or foundation.
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les .ij. chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse .i. jor ou .ij.;	and pull the head of the thread, and assemble the two pieces together, and tie one to the other, and leave them an inch or two;
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	And hold it no time, until the threads meet those cords that are between them, and intertwine;
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	Then treat the wound until it is healed and sanitized.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	If the fistula does not puncture, make an incision in all possible ways that you can, as long as it is not too deep.
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Indeed, it is not fitting to puncture through the placement so deeply, and then treat it, as we have said, until it is sanitized.
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	The form of the thin prickly tube through which one makes a fistula is quite small and consists mainly of;
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	And on another hand no, because one should not handle what one should not be handling, as you see here:
des emorroydes	from bleeding wounds
Emorrydes sont selonc ij. manieres: ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc,	Bleeding wounds occur in two ways: when they are inside the wound bed, like a piece of resin, and there may be small or large ones, and blood collects underneath them.
et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement; mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor,	And if there is one or more of them, they are removed from the base and at the head of the base; but those that are removed have little moisture.
et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	And sometimes even a little bit of yellow water or a little blood, and they have the color of a corpse.
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	And for the treatment of those who have them within the base, you instruct the patient to expel it through grooves until the bases come out and the threads are visible;
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	If you hurry, you pinch it with tweezers, or hold it with your nail, then scrape at its roots.
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a .i. drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	And if they cannot hold them due to their moisture, take them in two strips of cloth, or with cotton, or from a camel leather piece;
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	And pull them with your fingers, then pinch them, and dust them with some hot powders that are like fire cauterization;
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, puis les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	Or you can burn them as it is said or explained in the chapter about cauterization, and then treat them with other remedies until they heal.
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	And if the foundation cannot come out, you should burn the patient with the application of a blister-producing substance that is sharp to wash the one that is or has a foundation, so that it can come out completely;
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	If the organs fail to function, and if their tendons are strong at their foundation, then the treatment is light;
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	And you should take them with your fingernail or tongs, and cut them, then treat them in the way we have described, while they are still whole, fearing the metal cut by incision.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere: pren .i. fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les .ij. chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille,	It is necessary that you sew it in this manner: take a single twisted thread, and insert it into a needle, and then pull the thread through from above and make the needle pierce from another side, and loop the two ends of the thread over the needle together.
et si soit dou large; et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse .i. por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	and if it is wide; and tighten the thread properly, then tie the thread into a knot, and remove the needle, and do this with all others, and leave one for bleeding off excess blood;
puis met sus le fondement .i. drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	Then place on the foundation one piece of moist cloth in oil with rose or as a poultice, and place on the foundation, and instruct the patient to rest;
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and then leave it until it cools down, and when they are settled, if you treat with ointment and other treatments, as long as they have cooled off.
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	do the drying slowly in the ashes or on the ground.
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	Many times, there has been drying in the intestines, and due to the nature's constraint, and when the illness is old and medication no longer helps.
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	If it is necessary for you to set at the tip of a thorn or on your nail the bark above, which should not be left damp;
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;	then treat it until it becomes hard as it should;
et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	and if it does not become hard, then start scraping again with more force than before, until some healing begins, and it becomes scoured;
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat it until it is healed.
dou fremit	The tremble
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	Antennae are a small false appearance on the body, they extend forward;
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	And when you touch it moves coldly, and one feels it like a death tremble, spreading throughout the body, particularly more in the hands than elsewhere.
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	And the treatment involves taking a stick from a goose feather or a strong vulture feather and placing this stick on the tremble until the purple ring completely surrounds it.
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	Then turn your hand all along the cane until you grasp it completely by its trembling, and place it down fully, and eliminate its trembling from its roots.
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	And if you see it, do this with an arachnid or iron cane in the form as described, and make it slender everywhere and smooth above and below:
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	nor should it be pierced, for you must hold onto both ends and squeeze. And if you see any trembling, cauterize the tremor, just as it is shown in the section on cautery.
de la forme dou clistere	in the form of a bladder
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet; et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	No silver or hot iron, or molten spider or lead should ever be used. And these small and large instruments should not be employed according to who they are intended for.
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	Therefore, when treating children and those who are weak and painful, use small tools.
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	The shape of the tool being small and large as described above, or how you tie the belly according to this manner:
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez; et ait a l’un des costez .ij. pertus, et en l’autre .i.;	and there should be an opening where you tie the belly in such a way that you see it, and so that the head is pierced inside; and on one side of this have two holes, and on the other side one hole.
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus,	And let it be for the belly, where one places medicines of a beast's bladder or parchment, and pierce thoroughly with small pieces.
et ait entre chescun pertus .i. doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus .i. fil fort de fil crut tort en .x. ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	And place one inch of space between each piece, then insert a strong thread made from raw wool yarn in these pieces for an inch or about halfway through, and join the belly as if it were a goat.
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize; et c’est li forme dou cercle:	And when the medication is inside, bind it with a strong thread in front of the tool, then seal it; and this forms a circle:
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	And ensure the medication is neither too hot nor too cold, apply a layer of oil or yolk butter around the seal, or something similar, then gently place it.
puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses .ij. mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit,	Then the surgeon directs his two hands together on it while it's fully visible, then removes the cyst, and lifts the patient's legs at the sides.
et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet; et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	And if the medicine is meant to emerge, let it come out as much as possible; and if it sleeps for a whole night, then more help will be greater.
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you use the enema in a case of belly discomfort, and the medicine hastens to come out, then repeat it as long as he feels well.
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por .i. enfant;	And if there's bleeding from the anus or its root, or from a wound, then use the enema as thin as for a child of one year;
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	And this is the shape of a subtle knot beneath which the skin might be strained:
des plaies	of wounds
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies; or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	We have discussed the treatment of wounds in the division; now we will discuss treatments for hands and medicine, according to their completion.
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	I say that wounds are diverse depending on how they are made, and depending on where the wounds are located, and for what reason they were caused.
Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d’espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses;	The things which cause wounds are produced by the breaking of bone, and the slicing of a sword or knife, or from a lance or staff or axe, or from similar actions.
ou que sont faites selonc les leus dou cors, si com plaie que chiet sus le col, ou sus le chief, ou le peis, ou le ventre, ou le foie, et semblans membres;	or those which are made according to the body's parts, such as a wound that affects the neck, or head, or belly, or liver, and similar limbs;
et je vos dirai la cure de chescune plaie, et encomencerai as plaies dou chief simples, car li remenbrance venra en son chapistre.	and I will tell you the treatment for each wound, and start with wounds of the head that are simple, because the memory will come to its chapter.
Je dis que quant simple plaie vient ou chief, et li os n’est brisiez, si pren garde se c’est de gitement de piere ou de semblans choses, et li cuir est toutevoie rompus et est li plaie grans,	I say that when a simple wound comes or to the head and the bone is not broken, be careful if it's due to the breaking of stone or similar actions, and even though the skin has been torn completely, the wound is large,
et tu doutes levement d’aposteme chaut: si le fai tantost sainier de la cephalique meismement s’il vient poc de sanc de la plaie, et soit li sainie au contraire de la partie navree;	And if you slightly doubt about the abscess: if it produces a little blood from the wound immediately after treatment of the scalp in the same manner, and is treated oppositely to the retracted part;
et eschuisse li malaides repletion de vin et de viandes grosses.	And if you have excess malaise from drinking wine and eating heavy meats.
Et s’il ne vuet sainier, si soit amenuisie sa viande, et ne boive point de vin, ne ne menjuce point de char;	And if he does not wish to be treated, then reduce his food intake and do not give him wine or meat.
et met sor la plaie, se apostemes chaus i vient, coton moilliet en oile roset soulement, ou en vin stiptice;	And apply it to the wound, if abscesses appear and come out, use moist cotton in oil rose only, or in astringent wine.
et s’il n’i a aposteme chaut, si met sus la plaie, s’elle est fresche a tout son sanc, et elle n’est muee par l’air, poudre, que je dirai un poc ci aprés;	And if there is no pus present, then place on the wound, while it's fresh with all its blood, and it isn't disturbed by air, powder, which I will mention shortly;
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucuns oignemens, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the wound has been disturbed, then apply some remedies until it heals.
Et se li plaie est grans si com de tailleure d’espee et de semblans, et les levres ne se pueent assembler par tentes, si les assemble par cousture, si com je dirai as plaies dou ventre, de la costure.	And if the wound is large like that of a sword or similar, and the lips cannot be brought together by stitches, then join them through suture, as I will explain for wounds on the belly, from the suture.
Se li plaie est descoverte de l’os, et pent, et ne tient mais que a un poc, si le cope; puis cure la plaie de medicine, et restoure char dure en leu de cuir,	If the wound is exposed bone and flesh, and it only holds together with a little pressure, if you apply it. Then treat the wound with medicine, and restore hard tissue instead of skin,
et comande au malaide a mengier grosses viandes, si com testes et froment cuit, ausi com poulz, et semblans choses.	And instruct the patient to consume large meats, such as brains and cooked wheat, also like chickens, and similar items.
Et se tu trueves ou cuir porriture, et il n’aert a l’os, si cope lou porrit tot, et giete fuer, puis le cure;	And if you find rotten skin or it doesn't reach the bone, and it smells to the bone, then cut out the rot completely, and remove pus, then treat;
et se il ait artere en la plaie ou voine, dont sans cort, et il ne puet estainchier par medicines, si quier l’artere, et se tu la trueves desloie, si la lie d’un fil;	And if there is an artery in the wound or vein, which cannot be stopped by medicine, then cut out the artery, and if you find it dislocated, tie it with a thread.
et se ceu ne profite mie, si la cauterize.	And if this does not help, burn it.
Et se ces plaies sont petites et simples, si est li cure legiere: et est que tu mettes ens ceste poudre qui soude ainsois que li ars l’ait muee.	And if these wounds are small and simple, then the treatment is light: and you should put on this powder which sticks together in such a way that when the heat of the fire has applied it.
Et li maniere de la poudre si est: pren encens une partie; sanc de dragon .ij. parties; chalz vive .iij. parties, et le poudre subtilment,	And the way of the powder is thus: take part of incense; blood from a dragon two parts; live charcoal three parts, and finely ground,
et emple la plaie, et l’estraint forment, tant qu’elle s’aerse bien et se joigne a tout son sanc;	and apply it to the wound, and press it firmly until it is well ventilated and joins with all its blood;
et puis la lie bien, et la laisse sens desliier, s’elle n’enfle; car on n’oste la madicine tant qu’ele soit sanee.	and then properly cover it, and leave it to heal naturally if it doesn't swell; for the medicine is not removed until it is healed.
Et aucune fois fait on ceu de chalz soulement, quant on n’ait l’encens ne lou sanc de dragon, mais que li ars n’ait muee la plaie.	And one does not do this using charcoal alone, when one lacks the incense or the blood of dragon, but only when the surgeon has cleansed the wound.
Et se li ars ait mueit la plaie, meismement en esteit, si n’i met om mie ceste poudre;	And if the surgeon has cleaned the wound, indeed in that state, one does not add this powder;
mais met sus aucuns oignemens digestis, ou poulz de farine d’orge faites d’aigue et de miel, tant qu’ele giete bowe;	but apply some prepared dressings, or dough made from oat flour mixed with water and honey, as long as it is flowing.
puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	then continue with other treatments until the wound has healed.
Et se li brisure d’os vient avec la plaie, et elle est petite, si l’estrai as pinceures subtilz;	And if the bone fracture comes with the wound, and it is small, then use delicate probes to extract it;
et je vos dirai ci aprés les brisures dou chief.	and I will tell you about fractures of the head later.
de la plaie dou col	from the wound on the neck
Se plaie vient ou col et elle est simple, si n’a point de difference entre li et celi dou chief, mais se li ners dou col ou li artere est copee.	This wound occurs in the neck and it is simple, if there is no difference between it and those of the head, but if it affects the collarbone or the artery, then it is different.
Se c’est li ners, si n’i a autre engien que laissier la cure, et n’i mettre nulle chose restraignant, car il nuit as ners et les fait retraire;	If it's the nose, if there is no other tool, leave the treatment alone, and don't put anything restraining, because it harms the nose and makes them recede.
et ne mettre sus la plaie rien froit, car li substance des ners est froide, et li continuation d’aus si est avec le cerveil, qui est li plus haus membres;	and do not apply anything cold to the wound, for the substance of the nose is cold, and its connection to the brain is with the head which is the highest part of the body.
mais soit li medicine souez, si com chalz lavee en aigue douce, et mellee avec oile roset, et cucie lavee ausi en aigue douce,	but use medicine that is under (of the body), such as water in which rose oil has been washed and mixed with water used for washing cucumbers,
et autres pieres de mine selonc ceste maniere, et oignemens moistes.	and other minerals in this manner, and moist applications.
Et se li plaie est grans, si la cout et lie de bendes, puis la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the wound is large, then treat it by binding with cloths.
Et se les plaies sont parfondes et ele est chevee et pleinne de bowe, si la perce ou plus bas leu;	And if the wounds are deep and filled with pus, then puncture them or even further down.
et se li artere est copee, et decorremens de sanc en vient, si la desoivre, et la loie, et la cauterize se mestier est;	And if the artery is cut and blood begins to flow, then uncover it, and bandage it, and apply heat ( cautery ) if necessary.
et se li espinee de la gorge est copee, ou li keurs, et li conduiz est gardez, par coi la viande va,	And if the windpipe or lungs are cut, or the passage is disrupted by which food goes,
si cout le keur sus la cainne de la gorge, et ne touchier la gorge mais la remet selonc sa figure naturel;	if you heat the knife above the gullet's notch, and do not touch the throat but reset it according to its natural shape;
et puis l’estrain avenanment, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le cure d’oignemens desechans tant qu’il soit sanez;	and then set the protrusion, and leave it for several days, then treat with dry ointments until it heals;
et se li plaie a fait empression en l’os, si la quier;	and if the wound has made an impression into the bone, you should remove it;
et s’il i a pieces d’os, si les trai fuers toz se tu pues, et ces que tu ne pues avoir, si laisse tant que li plaie porrisse,	and if there are pieces of bone, try to extract them thoroughly, and if you cannot remove them all, let the wound heal until it fleshes over;
et soit desevree et aligie li issue;	And when it is drained and bound up is its treatment;
et se li plaie est fresche, si poudre sus la poudre que j’ai dit.	And if the wound is fresh, apply the powder I've mentioned on it.
Et s’il a en la plaie os et il i a fistule, si la cure ensi com j’ai dit en son chapistre.	And if there are bones and an opening in the wound, treat it as described in my chapter.
de la plaie de lance ou de coutel	from the wound of a spear or a knife
Se c’est cop de lance ou de coutel, et li plaie est parfonde, si regarde se de la plaie saut ventositez cant li malaides alainne: saiches adonques que li plaie est mortelz;	If it's blood from a spear or knife, and the wound is deep, then look at whether wind blows out of the wound: if this happens to the patient alone, you'll realize that the wound is mortal.
et s’elle n’est parfonde, et elle est fresche a tout son sanc, si n’i mettre mie a la premiere houre la poudre, ne ne la liier mie por le sanc que ne demorse em parfont,	And if it's not deep and its blood is flowing freely, then don't put any powder on it or bind it immediately for the fear that the blood would not stop flowing.
et reviegne au cuer, et ocie lou malaide;	Let him rest at his heart, and make him lie down;
mais i met oignement atractif, et le lie .ij. fois le jor;	but apply an attractive ointment, and bind it twice a day;.
et se tu n’as oignement, si met en la plaie viel coton por succier fuers la moistor,	And if you don't have ointment, place old cotton into the wound to absorb moisture.
et fai dormir le malaide sus la plaie .iij. jors, ou .iiij., ou plusors;	And make the patient rest on the wound for 3 days, or 4, or more;
si n’i venra mie spasme, ne tremor male de cuer n’es traingnemens d’alainne;	if no convulsions occur, nor severe heart tremors, nor sudden movements;
et quant tu vois les bones dispositions, si saiches que li plaie est sauve.	and when you see the good signs, you will know that the wound is saved.
Cure la donques de tentes et d’autres cures, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then treat with various remedies until the blood is cleansed;
et s’elle ne puet saner, et oevre, adés saiches que il i a fistule; si la cure si com on doit.	and if it cannot be healed and operated on, know that there will be a fistula; treat it as one should for such cases.
Et se li plaie est d’incision d’espee ou de coutel, et elle est simple, ou pis ou au dos, si la cure de ceu qui est devant;	And if the wound is from a sword or knife incision, and it is simple, or worse or on the back, follow the treatment of the one who was injured.
s’elle est grans, de cousture; et s’elle est petite, de poudre, et s’elle est empressee en l’os, et en a copeit pieces, si quier la plaie, et les trai fuers s’il sont desevrez;	And if it is large, stitch it up; and if it is small, use powder, and if it is embedded in the bone, or has pieces inside, identify the wound and remove any cleanable foreign objects.
et s’il ne sont desevrez, si laisse porrir la plaie, si aligera li estractions;	And if they are not drained, leave the wound to fester, facilitating the extractions;
et des autres plaies as autres membres est li jugemens si com nos avons dit.	And for other wounds on other limbs, the judgments are like what we have said.
dou derrompement dou ventre	about the rupture of the abdomen
Li derompemens dou ventre est grans et moiens et petis;	The ruptures of the abdomen come in large, medium, and small sizes;
de la grant plaie saut aucune fois li intestine, ou li ners des intestines, par coi li intromission d’aus;	From a large wound spring forth once again the intestines, or parts of the intestines, due to their introduction.
et li costure est plus malaisie, et aucune fois vaut pis li petite plaie que li grans,	And the stitches are more troublesome, and nothing beats a small cut compared to a large one,
por ceu c’on remet plus a poinnes les intestines en, s’on ne les i remet de chaut en chaut;	Because then we put the intestines back in less times, if we don't replace them little by little;
por ce que li intestine enflent tantost qu’il sentent le froit, si rentrent plus a poinnes,	For when the intestines swell as soon as they feel cold, if they are put back in less times,
et por ceu vaut mues li moieinne plaie, por ceu c’on ramoine mues l’intestine a son leu que as autres .ij.	And because this heals the half-dead wound, because we move the intestines to their place where the others are.
Et saiches que li routure dou ventre est selonc .iiij. manieres:	Know that there are four ways of a belly rupture:
les .ij. costures communes avienent en la costure dou ventre,	the two common stitches occur in the abdominal seam,
et li costure des autres plaies dou cors et .ij. autres costures propres sont communes as autres plaies;	and the stitches for other wounds in the body and the two other proper stitches are common to other wounds;
et toutevoie elles sont plus propres avec la costure dou ventre, et je dirai une chescune et declairerai.	And yet they are more accurate with the stitch along the belly, and I will say each one and clarify them.
Je di que quant li plaie est petite, et aucune chose de l’intestine ist fuer,	I say that when the wound is small, and nothing from the intestine has escaped,
et griés chose est dou remettre, ceu est par l’une des .ij. manieres:	And if there are injuries to be treated, this can be done in one of two ways:
ou por la petitece de la plaie, si com nos avons dit,	or because of the smallness of the wound, as we have said,
ou por ce que li intestine est enflez por le froit.	because the intestines are swollen due to cold.
Et quant il est frois, eschaufez lou en teil maniere:	And when he's cold, warm him up in this manner:
moillie une esponge ou .i. mol drapeil en aigue tede soulement,	dampen a sponge or use one part of clove oil in water only.
ou tu cuis en aigue squinant et cipre et spique,	or cook with boiling water that includes soap and pepper.
et arose l’intestine tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	And let the intestines grow until their swelling is cut out;
et aucune fois fait ce vins restraingnans, et est muedre que awe soule por desenfler.	And once this is done, make him drink so that he relaxes in order to relieve the swelling.
Et quant tu vois l’enfleure departir, si amoiste l’intestine d’aigue ou altee et malves soient cuites,	And when you see the swelling departing, moisten the intestines with water or broth that has been well cooked,
car par ceu est aligie li entree a poc de chose;	because this makes the entry able to accept little things;
et s’il n’i puet entrer, si fent un poc la plaie a l’estrument de coi on cope les emorroydes;	And if it cannot enter, they make a small incision with the tool used to remove blood clots;
et li premiere cure est muedre que li taille,	And the first treatment is to rub until the wound heals,
que nus n’i doit taillier sens grant necessiteit n’i ait;	which we should not cut without great necessity or if it is not needed;
et c’est li estrumens por le fendre:	and these are the tools for splitting them:
si trenche dedens en la corbeure et defuer non, et vez ci la forme:	If you cut inside the bend and not outward, and see this shape:
Et quant li plaie est enlargie, et li intestine saut fuer,	And when the wound is enlarged, and the intestines jump out,
si le remet arer selonc la forme naturel en son leu propre,	if you place it back according to its natural shape in its proper location,
se tu en as pooir, car ce vaut mues.	If you have the ability to do so, because this is valuable practice.
Quant li plaie est large, et elle est en la partie desoz lou ventre,	When the wound is wide, and it's located in the abdominal area,
si covient que tu faices gesir lou malaide sus son dos,	If you need to allow the patient to heal on their back,
et met ses jambes plus haut que son chief;	and place his legs higher than his head;
et s’elle est en la partie desoz le ventre,	And if it's in the belly region,
si met le chief et le pis plus haut que les parties desoz,	then place the head and the buttocks higher than the belly area.
et ausi se li routure dou ventre est en l’une des .ij. parties	and similarly, if there is a tear in the belly region at one of these two places,
si met t’entente en ceu que li partie navree soit plus haute que li autre;	then ensure that the torn part is higher than the other.
et ensi covient amenistrer ceu que je dis en plaies grans et moienes.	And so, one must administer what I say about large and medium wounds.
Es plaies petites met ceu que t’est apparilliet,	For small wounds, use what is suited to you.
puis aies entre tes mains .i. ministre pitous ki teigne toute la routure a sa main,	Then have at your disposal surgeons who can heal the entire wound with their hands,
et assemble les levres;	And gather the lips;
et c’est la maniere commune de costures,	And this is the common method of stitches,
et est que tu preignes une aguille ou plusors, selonc la quantiteit de la largesce de la plaie,	and you should use one needle or more, according to the width of the wound,
puis laisse des le chief de la plaie .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une aguille ou il ait .i. boin fil fort;	then start sewing from the edge of the wound about an inch away, and place one needle through the thread about half an inch thick;
et perce les .ij. chiés dou cuir avec les .ij. chiés dou siphac,	and pierce both sides of the skin with both needles through the flesh,
qui est desoz le cuir dedens, tant que tu la faices percier de celle partie,	which is beneath the skin, as long as you pierce it from that part,
et assemble les .ij. chief dou siphac les .iiij. ensamble;	and join them together so that all four main siphons come together;
puis l’estrain d’un fil double entor l’aguille de .ij. pars,	then stretch out one double thread around the needle from two sides,
puis assemble les .ij. chiés de la plaie avenanment,	and join the two edges of the wound with an addition,
et puis laisse .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une autre aguille;	And then leave one inch of space, and place another needle;
puis la lie dou fil si com tu as fait la premiere aguille,	then weave the thread in the same way you did with the first needle,
et ne cesser de ceu faire selonc ceu que tu as mestier des aguilles,	and continue doing this according to your skill with needles,
tant que toute li plaie soit restrainte;	until all the wound is held in place;
et soient les aguilles moienes, entre subtilz et grosses,	And let them be of moderate size, between fine and thick ones,
car les aguilles subtilz copent toute la char, et les trop grosses si ne pueent mie bien entrer:	because the very fine needles cut all the flesh, and the too thick ones do not enter well at all:
por ceu covient qu’elles soient moienes;	for this reason they should be of moderate size;
et ne covient mie bouter les aguilles trop au defuer de la char et dou cuir,	and needles should not be placed too far out from the flesh and skin,
