que li malaides n’estrangle; et le laisse jusc’au matin, que li plaie soit sanee.	That the sick person does not strangle themselves; and let them stay until morning, so that the wound heals.
De la sainie des leivres	Regarding the treatment of wounds
Li sainie des voinnes des levres desus si aident a cole en la bouche, et a corruption de gencives, et fendures de levres, et dou neis et entor.	The treatment of veins in the mouth aids in closing wounds and helps with gum decay, lip cracks, nosebleeds and internal injuries.
Et li qualitez de la sainie si est de faire seoir lou malaide devant toi, et estraint son col si com j’ai dit;	And the quality of this treatment involves having the sick person stay in front of you, restraining their neck as I have described;
puis torne la levre, et regarde as .ij. voinnes, dont l’une est a la destre levre et li autre a la senestre,	Then turn the lip and look between the two veins, one being on the right lip and the other on the left.
et les conoist on par ceu qu’elles sont noires, et par ceu que entor elles a voines menues noires:	And recognize them by their blackness, and because within them there are small black veins:
cope donques l’une et l’autre, et se tu ne les conois, et tu en es en doutance,	Tie both of them then, and if you do not know which one it is and you're in doubt,
si cope la plus grosse de chescune part, et tout ausi fai des .ij. voinnes que sont desus et desoz, car c’est une meisme maniere.	If the larger one of each side, and do the same for both veins above and below, because it is the same method.
De la sainie desoz la lengue	Of the treatment concerning the tongue
Li sainie des voinnes que sont desoz la lengue si aide aprés la sainie de la cephalique, et c’est a l’estrecement de la gorge, et as maladies de l’uve, et as maladies de la bouche;	The treatment of veins that are located on the tongue should assist after the treatment of the head, and it is at the narrowing of the throat, and concerning eye diseases, and concerning mouth ailments;
et li qualitez dou sainier si est que li malaides siece entre tes mains devant lou soleil, et li lieve la lengue, et regarde desoz en chescun costeit une voinne noire:	And the quality of a surgeon is that when the patient's body responds under your hands in front of the sun, and you lift the tongue, and look underneath on each side there is a black vein:
saine donques l’une et l’autre, et n’aler mie trop em parfont, car desoz sont les arteres.	Then it's healthy for both, but not too far inside either, because just below are the arteries.
Les voinnes dou coute dont on saine communement sont sainies selonc .ij. manieres:	The veins of the arm which are commonly treated, are treated according to two methods:
ou em poignant a tout .i. flaime mirtin large, ou olivaire subtil si com coutez trenchans, et est apelez «anesil»;	they apply either with a very wide iron flame or a thin olive one if the veins are deep and narrow, and they are called 'aneils';
et sont large et subtil selonc la largesce et l’estrecement des voinnes.	and are large and fine according to the width and narrowing of the veins.
Li forme dou flaime mirtin si est mout renommee, et est large si com tu vois:	The shape of the mirthin flame is very well known, and it is quite wide as you can see:
Et ait mestier por ovrir les voinnes chevees plaines de gros sanc apparent, et que contienent gros sanc et trouble;	And it requires to open veins filled with large visible blood, and those containing large blood and disturbance;
et c’est li forme dou flaime olivaire:	and this is the form of olive oil:
et est plus subtilz apointé, et est por sainier les voinnes subtilz, ou il a subtil sanc citrin.	and it is more penetrating, and used to cleanse delicate veins, or it has fine yellow blood.
Li sainie de la basilique, qui est une de ces voinnes, si aide as maladies que sont desoz la gorge, et ou col, et ou peis, et ou ventre;	The cleansing of the basilica vein, which is one of these veins, helps with diseases that affect the throat and neck, and the chest, and the stomach;
et covient au sainor qu’il saine saigement, et qu’il se warse de l’artere qui est desoz.	And it is necessary for the surgeon to heal wisely, and he must beware of the artery that is nearby.
Et s’il cope l’arterre, et decorremens de sanc vient, si le covient estainchier, si com j’ai dit;	And if he cuts into the artery, and a flow of blood ensues, it behooves him to staunch the bleeding, as I have said;
et ne doit mie estre poignans li flaime, mais taillans si com anesil.	and there should not be any tugging on the flame, but cutting in such a way as with rabbits.
Et se li basilique n’apert manifestement, si covient que tu l’estrainges, et chainge une autre;	And if the basilica does not open clearly, it is necessary to extract it and change another one;
ou tu quieres aucun rain de li, ou tu saine en leu de li la voinne emmi le bras: elle apert manifestement;	If you do not want any blood from him, or you open his vein at his arm: it clearly opens.
et la cope au flaime anesil, si com nos avons dit.	And apply the flame to the spot again as we said.
Et se tu vues conoistre le leu de la sainie, si covient ainsois que tu estraignes lou bras, que tu touches le leu tant que tu conoisses le poulz;	And if you know how to perform the operation, it is thus that you should straighten the arm, touching the place until you feel the pulse;
puis signe le leu d’enche, et puis lie lou bras, et cope la voine dou flaime anesil;	Then mark the site of insertion, and then fix the arm, and apply the flame to that spot again.
et warde que tu ne ferir en l’artere quant tu vois le leu enfleit, car c’est de l’artere: eschui la donques.	And make sure you do not cut into the artery when you see the limb inflates, for it is from the artery: listen to this then.
Et se tu vois saillir en haut ausi com l’urine d’un enfant, et li sans est rouges et subtilz, saiches que c’est sans de l’artere:	And if you see it protruding upwards like the urine of a child, and the veins are red and delicate, know that it is blood from an artery: be aware of this.
haste toi donques, et met ton doi sus longement, puis oste ton doi se li sans estainche, que maintes fois avient;	So hurry up then, and place your finger for a while, then remove your finger when the bleeding stops, as has often happened;
se lie lou bras, et laisse ensi, et ne lou mueve li malaides; et soit sus paour, et ne lou mueve tant qu’il soit sanez.	Fasten his arm, and leave it like that, do not move the patient; be cautious, and do not move until they are healed.
Et se li sans n’est estainchiez, et il te vaint, et li medicine ne t’est presens, si cope l’artere s’elle apert, car li chief de li retraient; et estainche li sans.	And if the wound is not cleaned, and you need it, and the medicine is not present, if you open the artery when it opens, because the head of the body retreats; and clean the wound.
Et pren une escorce de fistice, et la fent, et pren l’une des moitiez et lie sus bien jusc’a l’autre jor;	And take a bark of the horse chestnut, and cut it, and take one of its halves and bind it tightly until the other day.
se li sans estainche, c’est bien; se ce non, si le cure, si com nos avons dit, des poudres qui estainchent sanc;	If the wound is cleaned, that's good; if not, then treat it as we have said, with powders that clean blood.
et li estainchemens n’est mie griés em plusors dispositions por le petit leu de la plaie, et la possance dou liien dou bras.	And the wound's cleaning isn't troubled by various positions for the small area of the wound, and the strength of the arm connection.
Li sainie de la voinne em mileu si aide qu’elle trait sanc dou chief desus, et dou cors desoz,	The treatment of the vein involves assistance through bloodletting from the head up to the neck, and downwards towards the chest,
por ceu qu’elle est composte de la basilique et de la cephalique, si com nos avons dit;	Because it consists of the basilic vein and the head vein, just as we have said;
et covient au sainor qu’il se warse por lou nerf qui est desoz, et s’il point trop em parfont, et il trueve lou nerf,	And it's important for the surgeon to be cautious when it comes to the nerve that is nearby, and if he doesn't go far enough, and should find the nerve,
et il enfle et li santez soit griés, et par aventure ne puet saner;	And it inflates and harms the health, and by chance cannot heal;
et cist nerf apert mult de fois, et s’il n’apert en aucuns homes por sa subtiliteit, si covient que tu lou saines de l’estrument anesil; et eschui lou nerf a ton pooir.	And this nerve opens many times, and if it doesn't open in any humans due to its subtlety, you should cut off the healthy part of the instrument; and listen for the nerve with your power.
Et se il a voinne entre les .ij. ners, si la fent dou lonc.	And if there is a vein between the two nerves, make the incision long.
Li sainie de la cephalique si aide, qu’ele atrait sanc dou chief, et aide as eulz;	The treatment for headache helps, as it drains blood from the head, and aids in relieving pain;
et covient sainier em poignant au flaime olivaire ou au flaime mirtin, car c’est li plus sauve de toutes les voinnes, car il n’a desoz li ne nerf ne artere.	And it is advisable to treat with oil of the olive or oil of the myrtle, for this is the safest of all veins, because there is no obstruction from either nerve or artery.
Toutevoie, covient querir lou plus legier leu, et ne grieve rien s’on faut la premiere fois, et on rencomence;	In every way, it's important to seek the gentlest approach, and one shouldn't be dismayed if it needs to be done multiple times, instead just retry.
et par aventure enfle li leus a aucuns homes, cant on faut la premiere fois, mais il ne grieve rien.	And by chance, the limb may swell at certain points during the first attempt, but one shouldn't find it painful; rather, just retry.
La qualitez de la sainie si est selonc ta pensee.	The quality of health is according to your thought.
Li premiere chose que tu dois savoir de sainier, si est que sainie n’est amenistree fuer que por garder santeit,	The first thing you need to know about surgery is that medicine is managed with force only to preserve health,
et por eschuir les maladies a venir;	And to avoid future illnesses;
et soit li sainie faite en l’une des .iij. voinnes que sont ou coute: c’est a savoir, cephalique, faste, et basilique;	and let the healing be done in one of the three veins that are or cut: this means, the cephalic vein, the femoral vein, and the basilic vein;
et se doit on sainier en l’encomencement de prientens a geun, et en autompne et en yver aprés mengier, quant li signe de repletion aperent;	and let healing begin in the beginning of prayers on one's knees, and in autumn and after meals in winter, when the sign of fullness is seen;
et se doit on sainier le premier jor ou le tier, aprés .ij. houres ou .iij. dou jor.	and healing should be done on the first or third day, after two hours or three days.
Li sainie qui est aministree as maladies n’a point d’oure determinee, mais que quant besoing est de jor ou de nut, en toutes houres et en toz tens;	The treatment of diseases that is administered does not have a set time, but rather when need arises for day or nourishment, at all hours and in every situation;
et ne covient mie sainier les enfans jusc’a .xiiij. ans, ne femme portant fuer que des lou quart mois jusc’a septime.	And it is not proper to treat children until they are twelve and a half years old, nor for pregnant women only during the first quarter of their pregnancy up to seven months.
Ne ne se doient mie sainier li viel qui ont passez .lx. ans.	Neither should doctors treat the elderly who have surpassed sixty years old.
Et quant aucuns se vuet sainier, en quel maniere que ce soit, si covient k’il mondefie les intestines d’un clistere legier,	And when anyone wants to be treated, in whatever way, it is necessary that they cleanse their intestines with a gentle cathartic.
s’il a mout de fiens retenut, si que les voines n’atraient des intestines les superfluitez porries nuisans as membres principelz;	If there are some fats retained, so that the veins draw off the unnecessary stuff from the intestines harmful to the main body parts;
ne ne se saine mie cil qui est trop saolez de viandes, ne qui est yvres, tant k’il en soit fuer, ne ydropiques;	None recovers who is too full of meat, or drunk, as long as he is strong, or dropsical;
et se warse on de sainier aprés colique passion, et vomissement, et decorrement de ventre, et multipliement d’abiter a femme, et de traval, de veiller et de juner, et ceu que tot la vertu, ou par chose de l’arme ou dou cors;	And if someone is healthier after colic pain, and vomiting, and abdominal discomfort, and frequent urination, and laboring work, staying awake and being anxious, and that which quickly loses its strength, or due to something from the arm or injury to the body;
puis subtilie les humors, se li sans est gros, par viandes et par bevraiges et par medicines, se tu en as lou poir;	Then refine the fluids, if they are excessive, through meat and drinks and medicines, if you have the power;
puis entre ou bain, s’aucune chose ne lou deffent, por subtiliier lou sanc,	Then in or through a bath, if there's no resistance or obstruction, to thin out the blood.
et te saine de la voinne dou pis entor la tierce, si com nos avons dit;	and heal from the wound down towards the buttocks for three quarters of their length, as we have said;
et te garde celui jor de travail, et de poinne, et de luxure, et de semblans choses;	and keep that day free of work, and pain, and lust, and similar matters.
et soies liez et joians, et soit li sainieres plus haut que cil cui on saine, et li frote lou bras .ij. fois ou .iij.,	and bind and rest, and have the healers higher than those being healed, and rub the arm twice or three times.
puis estraigne lou liien desus moienement, car quant il est trop estrois ou poc, si ne puet corre li sans;	Then adjust it halfway above the link, because when it is either too tight or too loose, you cannot correct it without;
et puis le frote le leu as mains, tant que les voines enflent, et les sente on;	And then rub the area with your hands until the veins swell and one can feel them.
puis moille li sainieres le flaime d’un poc d’oile viel, puis mette son doit de sa main senestre sus celle voinne desoz lou leu un poc ou il vuet sainier,	Then moisten the wick of the lamp with a little old oil, then place your left thumb on that vein above the area a bit where he wants to cauterize.
que li voinne ne fue et faille au ferir.	so that the vein does not burn and rupture upon contact with the iron.
Car il i a voinnes que fuient ausi com cordes au sainier, et si a de telz que sont plainnes de ventositeit,	For there are veins that flow like strings under the skin, and some have such qualities of being full of windiness,
si que quant on met sus le flaime, si retrait a flaime, et ne puet ovrir li voinne, et ensi est on de ceus;	so that when one places them over the flame, they retract towards the flame, and cannot open the vein, and thus one is among those;
et s’il aoevre la voinne, si est li plaie trop estroite, por ceu si covient que li sainieres soit avisez en ces choses.	and if it opens the vein, the wound becomes too narrow, for in these matters one must be aware of what surgeons are regarding such things.
Et se li voine oevre la premiere fois, c’est boin; se ceu non, si rencomence ancor un poc desoz celui leu ou sus hastanment, se li leus n’est enflez.	And if the vein opens on the first try, that's good; but if not, it should be tried again slightly over where you were or quickly, depending on whether his arm is swollen.
Et se li leus est enflez, et li malaides s’espoante, se li laisse .i. jor ou .ij., et ne liier mie le bras:	And if your arms are swollen, and the veins stand out, let it be for one or two days, and do not bind the arm:
par aventure i venra apostemes chaus; ne n’entre ou bain, puis rencomence la sainie s’elle li plait;	By chance some pus will come out; don't enter water baths, then restart washing if it pleases her;
et se li pertuis est petis, ou li sans cort subtilment et tu doutes qu’il n’isse mie tant de sanc com tu vues, si fier en celui pertuis meisme a tout le flaime droitement;	And if the wound is small, or if it bleeds slightly and you doubt that not enough blood escapes as you see, so fix this in the very same wound to all the flame straightly;
et l’uevre un poc hastanment, ainsois que li leus soit enflez; car ceu avient maintes fois, quant li plaie est petite.	And let it heal a bit quickly, in such a way that your arm is swollen; because this happens many times, when the wound is small.
Se tu vois le leu enfleit, si ne rencomencier mie la sainie, et met sus un poc de lie d’oile, car elle alige lou cors dou sanc, et est muedre en cest leu li lie que li oile;	If you see the limb is inflamed, do not restart the healing process again, and place a little bit of olive oil on it, for she lightens the body from blood, and heals in that area where the oil is placed.
et ensi aministre la lie de oile en chescune sainie que tu saines les voines, por estanchier lou cours dou sanc;	and thus administer the olive oil in each healing you do to the veins, to stop the flow of blood;
et ceu meisme fait triaicle et bowe d’eus, quant on le met sus le leu; si subtilie li sans et s’espart quant il est trop gros.	And similarly make vinegar and wine, when you apply it to the limb; if the veins are too large, their fluid escapes.
Et s’il i vient uns apostemes gros, qui avient maintes fois, meismement quant il n’est sainiez fuer que a celi fois ou li overture de la voinne est petite,	And if there comes an abscess that is large, which happens often, even when it has not been treated before because the opening of the vein was small,
si te haste, et met sus le leu esponge moillie en aigue et en seil un poc chaut, et l’estraint une houre;	If you're in a hurry, place a damp sponge on your head and leave it for half an hour in water and wine that has been gently heated.
et covient que tu faices ceu aprés l’issue dou sanc de la voinne, et s’il demoure au leu aprés aucuns jors aucune noiror ou verdor, si ne li nuist mie;	It is necessary that you do this after the blood issue from the vein, and if it remains in place for several days with no signs of blackness or greenness, then it does not harm it.
et se tu vues, met sus aucune chose de aloes ou de mirre remise en jus de calament, monstastre, ou semblant.	And if you notice this, place on any substance made from aloes or myrrh in a solution of comfrey, mustard, or something alike.
Et maintes fois avient aposteme et aparance a la sainie de la basilique: met donques ta main sus, et se tu trueves le leu mol a la compression de la main, si est celle aparance male.	Many times abscesses and signs of healing were seen in the region of the basilica: so place your hand there, and if you find the area soft upon pressing with your hand, then that is an ill sign.

But if his veins are black, let him bleed until the blood turns red; and if you see a lot of it, let him bleed until it becomes thin; and if it is too hot, let him cool down.

Li voinne emmi le bras est sainie en leu de la voine dou chief por ceu qu’elle est composte.	The vein is located under the neck from the vein of the arm because it is composed that way.
Et li maniere de la sainie si est que li malaides boute sa main en aigue chaude, tant que li foscile soit rouges;	And the method of the treatment involves having the patient immerse his hand in hot water, until the veins turn red.

Li sainie de la salvatele de la main destre si vaut a toutes les maladies dou foie, et c’est li maniere:	The treatment for saving the right hand from all diseases of the liver is as follows:

et n’aler mie trop em parfont, car li nerf sont desoz toz desnuez de char,	and do not go too far in the application because all nerves are completely without flesh,

Li sainie de li en la main senestre si vaut a la maladie de la mice, et fai tout ausi com je t’ai dit devers destre.	The health of his left hand is against the disease of the mouse [a type of poisoning], and do everything similarly as I have told you for the right side.
Li sainie de la sophene si vaut a toutes les maladies que sont desoz le cors,	The strength of wisdom saves from all diseases that are within the body,
si com maladies de la marris, et retenement de flors, et maladie des rains, et des cuixes et des jambes ancienes, et semblans maladies.	If diseases of the liver, and retention of flowers (likely referring to blood or plant parts), and disease of kidneys, and old illnesses of hips and legs, and similar diseases.

saine la donques ou plus large rain, ou a la cheville, que mues vaut.	So in health or even more so in larger kidneys, or at the ankle, than if one considers.

ne ne douter de nerf, si com nos avons dit, et ensi fai de la sophene de l’autre piet igalment.	Do not doubt about nerves as we have said before and do the same for the other bone.

Des sainies de ventouse	Regarding suction healings
Ventouses sont fait de cornes, ou d’arain, ou de voirre; et ventosation si est faite selonc .ij. manieres: ou par ferir et atraire sanc, ou sens ferir.	Ventouses are made of horns, or spiders, or glass; and suction treatment is done in two ways: either by cutting and drawing blood, or without cutting.
Et ceste ventosation qui est sens ferir si est selonc .ij. manieres: ou elle est a tout feu, ou sens feu;	And this kind of suction which can cause injury is done in two ways: either immediately with heat, or without heat;
et ventosation qui est faite par ferir et par estraction de sanc si est faite en .xiiij. leus dou cors,	and this suction that is made by causing injury and extracting blood is done in 13 different ways within the body,
de coi li uns est tout en som le chief; et li autres est emmi le col;	because some are entirely in the head; and others are in the neck.
et .ij. autres en .ij. costeis dou col; et li ventouse desoz lou menton;	and two others are on both sides of the neck; and the suction cup under the chin.
et li ventouse des .ij. espaules; et li ventouse sus les crupies;	And the suction for both shoulders; and the suction over the hives;
et les ventouses emmi les .ij. bras; et les ventouses des .ij. jambes;	And the cups on both arms; and the cups on both legs;
et les ventouses des .ij. chevilles; et li ventosation ne trait point de sanc, fuer que des menues voinnes que sont esparses en la char,	And the suction on both ankles; and cupping does not target blood, but only small veins that are scattered in the flesh,
et por ceu n’en afoiblist om mie, si com on fait de sainie de voinne;	and because of this it did not weaken me at all, as one would do for the health of veins;
et ne covient mie qu’elle soit aministree, ne a tout feu ne sens feu, en aucune maladie qui vient de repletion, tant que toz li cors soit vuidiez.	And it should not be administered, nor with any fire or by any means, in any disease that comes from overfullness, until all the organs have been emptied.
Et se par necessiteit de maladies covient ventoser, ou por acostumances, si l’amenistrons chescune houre en l’encomencement dou mois, ou en la fin, et emmi et en chescun tens;	And if it is necessary due to the disease to use suction or as a routine practice, we should apply it each hour at the start of menstruation, or at the end, and throughout and in every period;
car il i a de telz qui, quant il ont mestier de ventoser, si ont pesant chief;	because there are those who, when they need to use suction, weigh themselves first;
et si a telz qui truevent repletion et roujor en lor faice, et en lor chief, et au col, et tenebrour as eulz;	and for those who find congestion and redness in their face, head, neck, and eyes;
et telz qui truevent une goute de sanc en lor bouche, et ont enflee la lengue, et raichent sanc;	And those who find a drop of blood in their mouth, and have lost their tongue, and cough up blood;
et si i a de telz qui songent, et voient par nut sanc et navrez et mors et semblans choses.	And if there are any such people who fear, and see through the nose blood, bones and similar things.
Et quant nos voions ces signes, et meismement quant c’est emmi lou mois, nos lou commandons a ventoser aprés .iij. houres dou jor.	And when we see these signs, especially around the end of the month, we instruct to suck after three hours each day.
Li sainie de la muze si aide a la grieteit dou chief … que vient as eulz, et ne covient mie que ce soit aprés l’evacuation de tout lou cors;	The health of the throat helps with the pain in the head... that comes from the eyes, and it is not right for it to be after the elimination of everything from the body;
et ceste ventosation si est en leu de la sainie de la cephalique,	This suction therapy is used for the health of the head,
et ne covient mie que cil qui est de froide complexion en use, ou qui ait chatharre, car ce lor fait mout grant nuisement;	And it should not be used by those who have a cold constitution, or who are having purging symptoms, for it causes much harm in these cases;
et por ceu ne covient mie que li veillart en usent, ne qui ont ou chief froides maladies.	And nor should they use this who have ear problems, nor those with cold head diseases.
Et cil qui s’en saine sovent, si devient oblious, et por ce covient mettre la ventouse un poc plus aval par la doutance d’obliance.	And those who often use this, become forgetful, and because of that, it's advisable to place the suction cup slightly further down due to the risk of forgetfulness.
Li ventosation emmi le col est en leu de la sainie dou chief et de la basilique, et por ceu vaut elle a l’estrecement dou pis,	Ventilation of the chest is located under the healthful part of the head and the basilica, and because of this it matches well with compression of the base.
et a fendure de la chenal dou pormon, et a toust, et a repletion;	and in making cuts down to the heart's channel, and immediately, and in recovery;
et la covient poc bouter, car s’elle tient trop fermement, si enjanre obliance ou stomac et ou cuer.	And it should not be pressed too much, for if she holds too tightly, she may cause obstruction or stomach and heart.
Li ventosations as .ij. costelz dou col si vaut as dolors dou chief, et obtalmie et emigrainne, et a l’estranglement, et a la dolor as racines des dens,	Ventilation at two points under the chest relieves head pain, eye diseases and toothaches, as well as choking, and pain in the roots of teeth.
et est en leu de la sainie de la basilique; et covient que tu comandes au sainor qu’il espresse sa main au mettre, qu’il ne cope l’artere, et ne veigne decorremens de sanc.	And it is in the area of the healing of the basilica; and you should instruct the healer to extend their hand during the operation, not to touch the artery, and not let blood flow repeatedly.
Li ventosations desoz lou menton si vaut a maladie de bouche, et a corruption de gencives, et semblans maladies qui sont en la bouche; et est en leu des sainies des .ij. levres.	The ventilation under the chin contributes to mouth diseases and gum decay, as well as similar illnesses occurring in the mouth; it is within the field of healing for the two lips.
Li ventosations des espaules vaut a maladie que vient de chalor et de remplissement.	The ventilation under the shoulders leads to illness that comes from heat and congestion.
Li ventosations des coutes si vaut autant com des .iij. voinnes dou bras,	Ventilation under the elbows is equivalent to three veins of the arms,
car elle atrait sanc de ces grosses voinnes;	for it has blood from these large veins;

Li ventouse qui est sus la croupe si vaut as emoroydes dou fondement, et as maladies desoz, et covient que li ventouse soit grans, et soit d’arain, qu’elle a mestier de bien traire; et par aventure, s’elle estoit subtilz, si briseroit; et i fai grans plaies.	The suction cup on the buttocks is good for drawing out dampness from deep within and various diseases from below. It's necessary that the suction cup be large and made of spider material; otherwise, if it were too fine, it might break and cause significant injuries.
Les ventouses des jambes si sainent apertement, car elles atraient sanc de tout le cors, et valent as dolors ancienes des rains, et de la marris, et de la vessie, et ramoinnent les flors; et sont en leu des .ij. sophenes, et des .ij. chevilles, et toutevoie elles afoiblissent lou cors aprés lonc us, et font venir paumison em plusors dispositions.	Leg suction cups should be used without hesitation, as they draw blood from the entire body and are beneficial for old pain in the legs, joints, bladder, and kidneys, as well as eliminating toxins; they are placed on both ankles and calves, and eventually weaken the body after prolonged use, leading to emaciation.
Li maniere de mettre la ventouse si est que tu la mettes premier vuide, et succe tempreement, et la met hastanment, et remue igalment, et ne cesser de ceu faire, tant que tu voies lou leu rouge et enfleit, et apere li roujor dou sanc; puis fier, et remet les ventouses, et pren warde en la disposition des cors, car il i a telz qui ont tanre char, et clers porez: si covient ferir une fois soulement, et covient faire larges plaies, et un poc parfondes; et suce legierement.	The method of applying the suction cup is as follows: you should place it first when empty, and apply sucking steadily, then quickly, equally moving it, without stopping this action until you see the color red and swelling appear. Then stop for a moment, and replace the suction cups, taking care with positioning since there are those who have tough flesh and clear pores: they require only one strike and large wounds that go slightly deep should be made; and sucking should be done lightly.
Et se li sans est gros, si couvient ferir .ij. fois: la premiere fois por subtiliier la voie dou sanc gros.	And if the spot is large, then it's necessary to strike twice: the first time to delicately clear the way for thicker blood.
Et se li sans est tres espés, si covient ferir la tierce fois; et quant nos volons traire dou sanc poc et poc, si nos soffist soulement une fois.	And if the spot is very thick, then it's necessary to strike three times; and when we wish to draw out blood gradually, then we should only do so once.
Et se nos volons mout de sanc, si rencomensons sovent; et se li sans est espés, si fier em parfont, et li termines si est que li keurs soit perciez soudement,	And if we wish to remove much blood, we often continue; and if the wound is deep, we pierce it thoroughly, and the ends are such that the wounds are pierced suddenly.
et couvient a celui qui a gros cuir et dur, et qui ont estrois porelz, que tu oignes les leus des ventouses d’oile aperitif et dissolutif:	And it is necessary for that person who has thick skin and is firm, who has hardened veins, that you apply the limbs to the suction cups where they are pitted and corrosive:
se c’est en esteit, d’oile violet, ou d’oile d’amandres douces, ou d’oile de semence de cucurbite;	if it is in the purple oil, or sweet almond oil, or oil of pumpkin seeds;
et se c’est en yveir, d’oile de cresson, ou de lis, ou de camomille, ou autre semblant.	or if it's yellow, with spinach oil, or lily oil, or chamomile, or any other similar.
Et se li superfluitez est grosse et froide, si pren oile amaratin, ou de balsamite, ou oile d’anet, et les semblans.	And if the excess is large and cold, take oil of wormwood, or balsam, or anise oil, and similar remedies.
